These queries should all belong to the same datasource.\n   217→func buildErrorResponses(err error, queries []*simplejson.Json) splitResponse {\n   218→\ter := backend.Responses{}\n   219→\tfor _, 312→\t\t\t}\n   313→\t\t}\n   314→\t}\n   315→}\n   316→\n   317→// Hop-by-hop headers. These are the headers defined by the\n   320→// obsoleted RFC 2616 (section 13.5.1) and are used for backward\n   321→// compatibility.\n   322→//\n   323→// Copied from https://github.com/golang/go/blob/dc04f3ba1f25313bc9c97e728620206c235db9ee/src/net/http/httputil/reverseproxy.go#L171-L186\n   324→var hopHeaders = []string{\n   325→\t\"Connection\",\n   326→\t\"Proxy-Connection\", // non-standard but still sent by libcurl and rejected by e.g. google\n   327→\t\"Keep-Alive\",\n   328→\t\"Proxy-Authenticate\",\n   329→\t\"Proxy-Authorization\",\n   330→\t\"Te\",      // canonicalized version of \"TE\"\n   331→\t\"Trailer\", // not Trailers per URL above; https://www.rfc-editor.org/errata_search.php?eid=4522\n   332→\t\"Transfer-Encoding\",\n   333→\t\"Upgrade\",\n   334→\t\"User-Agent\",\n   335→}\n   336→\n   337→// removeHopByHopHeaders removes hop-by-hop headers.
